 tippaniyan He says, "looking at Sadashiv, i got the idea that he is only 57-58 years old and how old he looks

 Today is the 87th birth anniversary of the country's former President and Bharat Ratna awarded scientist and engineer APJ Abdulkalamki
 unka puraa naam awul pakir janullabdin abdul kalam tha
 He was born on 15 October 1931 in Rameswaram in the south Indian state of Tamil Nadu
 unke pita peshey se navik the or padhe- likhe nahin the
 He used to rent boats to fishermen
 paanch bhai or paanch bahanon vaale parivaar ko chalaane ke liye pita ke paise kam pad jate the isliye shuruaati shiksha jari rakhane ke liye kalam ko akhbaar bechney kaa kaam bhi karnaa padaa
 Kalam was always ahead to support the family
 bataaden, kalam saal 2002 se 2007 tak 11wein raashtrapati ke rup main desh kii seva kii
 Kalam, known as Missile Man, was a man full of ideas related to the progress and development of the country
 
 
 
 Know what kind of childhood, Kalam used to get up at 4 in the morning from the age of eight and go to take a bath in mathematics
 subah naha kar jane ke peeche kaaran yah tha ki prayek saal paanch bacchon ko muft main ganit padhaane vaale unke teacher bina nahaye aae bacchon ko nahin padhaate the
 After coming from tuition, he used to offer Namaz and after that he used to distribute news papers at Rameswaram railway station and bus stand till eight in the morning
 
 
 
 When arrived Isro arrived in Kalamisaro in 1962
 inhen ke project diarector rahete bharat ne apana pehla swadeshi upgrah prakshepan yaan eselvi-3 banaaya
 In 1980, the Rohini satellite was placed near the Earth's orbit and India became a member of the International Space Club
 kalam ne iske baad swadeshi gided missile ko dizin kiya
 They made missiles like Agni and Prithvi with Indian technology
 1992 se 1999 tak kalam raksha mantri ke raksha salaahkaar bhi rahe
 During this time, the Vajpayee government also conducted nuclear tests for the second time in Pokhran and India joined the nuclear weapon producing countries
 kalam ne vijan 2020 diya
 Under this, Kalam gave special thinking to India by cutting edge by 2020 through the advancement in science
 kalam bharat sarkaar ke mukhya vaigyanik salaahkaar bhi rahe
 In 1982, Kalam was made the director of DRDL (defense Research Development Laboratory)
 usee dauraan anna uniwarsity ne unhen doctor kii oopaadhi se sammanit kiya
 Kalam then gave the Defense Minister's scientific advisor, Dr
 vies arunachalam ke saath integrated gided missile deveopment program (ijmdipi) kaa prastaav taiyaar kiya
 a committee was formed under the chairmanship of Kalam for the development of indigenous missiles
 iske pehle charan main jameen se jameen par madhyam duuri tak maar karne vaali missile banane par jor tha
 In the second phase, it was proposed to make ground-to-air missiles, antitank missiles and the Reintree Experiment Launch Vehicle (rex)

 On the other hand, Hindutva has always been proud that Hindu may be considered impure within Hinduism, but birth is superior to all
 islam kii vah kattarta ki hamaara vahi rup thik he jise nabi ne parivartit kiya tha or hindutv kaa yah aagrah ki dharm ke maamle main hamen kisi se kuch siikhnaa nahin he, ye donon baaten diwaar banakar islam or hindutv ke bich khadi hai

 iphone yugers kii hameshaa se ek pareshaani rahi he ki unke smartphone main whatsapp lock nahin hota
 There is no whatsapp lock feature for Android as well, but there are dozens of third party apps on the Play Store
 in ap ke jariye android yugers watsap lock karte hai
 The iphone did not have this feature, there are hardly any apps found on the App Store that lock whatsapp
 lekin in par bharosaan nahin kiya ja saktaa
 To ease this problem, whatsapp has now introduced a lock feature for ios users
 yah sabhi ios yugers ke liye jari kar diya gaya he
 If you use iphone, then update your whatsapp from the App Store
 varjan 2
 19
 20 main lock feechar joda ja chukaa he
 Whatsapp lock works in different ways
 phase idi or tach idi
 For Face ID lock, you must have a smartphone from iphone X, XS, XS Max and XR
 tach idi jin yphone main he wo yugers tach idi se whatsapp analock kar sakate hai
 To activate this new feature, first of all you have to update whatsapp
 iske baad watsap settings main ja kar Privacy select karen
 Screen Lock will be seen in the last one here
 yahaan tap karte hi Require Face ID / Touch ID dikhegaa
 Now there are four options available here
 in opshans main Immediately sabase upar he or iske baad 1 minute, 15 minute or 1 ghante kaa opshan he
 These options mean how long you would like to keep whatsapp without lock
 sabase pehle opshan ko select karne par har baar watsap open karne ke liye aapako phase idi yaa tach idi kii jarurat hogi
 Whereas in the second option, whatsapp will be locked after some time
 watsap ke mutabik agar aapane watsap lock bhi kar rakhaa he phir bhi agar notification main koi massej dikhataa he to aap bina analock kiye hi use riplai kar sakate hai or pard sakate hai
 So, keep this in mind
 report ke mutabik android yugers ke liye bhi aise hi feechar kii testing kii ja rahi he
 Let us tell you that whatsapp has tested whatsapp Pay in India and this option will also be visible in whatsapp
 lekin isfiture ko aadhikariktor par launch nahin kiya gaya he, kyonki abhi watsap ko sarkaar kii taraf se clearence chahie
 Paytm and other companies have said that whatsapp payment cannot be secure, as no login ID password is required to open whatsapp
 ye bhi ek vajah ho sakati he ki watsap ne ab lock feechar laayaa he
